PART I : SEC. (I) - GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA - 10.02.2014
1 A
(Published by  Authority)
PART I : SECTION (I)  — GENERAL
Government Notifications
 PROVINCIAL COUNCILS  ELECTIONS ACT,  NO. 2  0F  1988
Notice under Section 22(1)
ELECTION  OF  MEMBERS  FOR  THE  WESTERN
PROVINCE  PROVINCIAL  COUNCIL  FROM  THE  ADMINISTRATIVE  DISTRICT  OF  COLOMBO
NOTICE is hereby given under section 22(1) of the Provincial Councils Elections Act, No. 2 of 1988 that the above election is contested
and that a Poll will be taken between 7.00 a.m. and 4.00 p.m. on 29 th March, 2014 and that -
(a) the names of the Candidates (as indicated by the Candidates) of each Recognized Political Party or Independent Group
placed in alphabetical order in Sinhala, for election as members of the above-mentioned Provincial Council, the serial
number assigned to each such Candidate and the approved symbol allotted to each such Party or Group and the
distinguishing number allotted to each Independent Group ; and
(b)  the situation of the Polling Station or Stations for each of the Polling Districts in the Administrative District and the
particular Polling Stations if any reserved for female voters
 are as specified in the schedule below.
2. The order in which the nemes of each Recognized Political Party and the distinugishing number of each Independent
Group appear in the Schedule shall be the same order in which these particulars will be printed on the ballot paper
H.T. K
AMAL PATHMASIRI,
Returning Officer,
Administrative District of Colombo.
District Secretariat,
Colombo.
10th February, 2014.
EXTRAORDINARY
The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka

PROVINCIAL  COUNCILS  ELECTIONS  ACT,  No.  2  OF  1988
Notice under Section 22(1)
ELECTION  OF  MEMBERS  FOR  THE  WESTERN  PROVINCE  PROVINCIAL  COUNCIL  FROM  THE
ADMINISTRATIVE  DISTRICT  OF GAMPAHA
NOTICE is hereby given under Section 22(1) of the Provincial Councils Elections Act, No. 2 of 1988 that the above election is
contested and that a Poll will be taken between 7.00 a.m. and 4.00 p.m. on 29th March, 2014 and that —
(a) The names of the Candidates (as indicated by the Candidates) of each Recognized Political Party or
Independent Group placed in alphabetical order in Sinhala, for election as members of the above-mentioned
Provincial Council, the serial number assigned to each such Candidate and the approved symbol allotted to
each such Party or Group and the distinguishing number allotted to each Independent Group ; and
(b) The situation of the Polling Station or Stations for each of the Polling Districts in the Administrative District
and the particular Polling Stations if any reserved for female voters ;
are as specified in the Schedule below.
2. The order in which the names of each Recognized Political Party  and the  distinguishing  number  of each  Independent
Group appear in the Schedule shall be the same order in which these particulars will be printed on the ballot paper.
J. J. R
ATHNASIRI,
Returning Officer,
Administrative District of Gampaha.

Gampaha,

PROVINCIAL  COUNCILS  ELECTIONS  ACT,  NO. 2 OF 1988
Notice  under  Section 22 (1)
ELECTION OF MEMBERS FOR THE WESTERN PROVINCE PROVINCIAL COUNCIL FROM THE
ADMINISTRATIVE DISTRICT OF KALUTARA
NOTICE is hereby given under section 22 (1) of the Provincial Councils Elections Act, No. 2 of 1988 that the above election is
contested and that a Poll will be taken between 7.00 a. m. and 4.00 p. m. on 29th March, 2014 and that –
(a) the names of the Candidates (as indicated by the Candidates) of each Recognized Political Party or Independent
Group placed in alphabetical order in Sinhala, for election as members of the above mentioned Provincial Council,
the serial number assigned to each such Candidate and the approved symbol allotted to each such Party or
Group ; and the distinguishing number allotted to each Independent Group ; and
(b) the situation of the Polling Station or Stations for each of the Polling Districts in the Administrative District and
the particular Polling Stations if any reserved for female voters,
are as specified in the Schedule below :
2. The order in which the names of each Recognized Political Party and the distinguishing number of each Independent
Group appear in the Schedule shall be the same order in which these particulars will be printed on the ballot paper.
U. D. C. J
AY ALAL,
Returning Officer,
Administrative District of Kalutara.
District Secretariat,
Kalutara,
10
